  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_193c9ce5-f529-44d7-a6d6-93109fac74be'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer7709582509490760734">Colleen Hoover, the <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author of <i>Maybe Someday</i> brilliantly brings to life the story of the wonderfully hilarious and charismatic Warren in a new novella, <i>Maybe Not</i>.<br/><br/>When Warren has the opportunity to live with a female roommate, he instantly agrees.   <span id="freeText7709582509490760734" style="display:none">Colleen Hoover, the <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author of <i>Maybe Someday</i> brilliantly brings to life the story of the wonderfully hilarious and charismatic Warren in a new novella, <i>Maybe Not</i>.<br /><br />When Warren has the opportunity to live with a female roommate, he instantly agrees. It could be an exciting change.<br /><br /><i>Or maybe not.</i><br /><br />Especially when that roommate is the cold and seemingly calculating Bridgette. Tensions run high and tempers flare as the two can hardly stand to be in the same room together. But Warren has a theory about Bridgette: anyone who can hate with that much passion should also have the capability to love with that much passion. And he wants to be the one to test this theory.<br /><br />Will Bridgette find it in herself to warm her heart to Warren and finally learn to love?<br /><br />Maybe.<br /><br /><i>Maybe not.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="7709582509490760734" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">The story is set partly before and partly during Maybe Someday, with Warren and Bridgette as the main characters. You will not see anything about Sydn<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">The story is set partly before and partly during Maybe Someday, with Warren and Bridgette as the main characters. You will not see anything about Sydney and Ridge after Maybe Someday, but you will see them in scenes you also read in Maybe Someday, just from Warren's point of view.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1122847603" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15704249236210422190"> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417672116i/12473945.jpg' width='400' height='230' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Well, this sure wasn’t boring or slow-kill-me-now paced. There were many ‘lol-worthy’ moments, dialogs and scenes for certain. This novella honestly doesn’t contain exactly my kind of humour or chemistry between characters, so it didn’t make me laugh or swoon, but entertaining is what it was never the less and, if you enjoyed <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17788403.Maybe_Someday__Maybe___1_' title='Maybe Someday (Maybe, #1) by Colleen Hoover' rel='nofollow noopener'>Maybe Someday</a>, then there are good chances this will please you very much. And, thank goodness, there is no love-triangle. It in fact follows the relationship between Warr</span>
  <span id="freeText15704249236210422190" style="display:none"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417672116i/12473945.jpg" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, this sure wasn’t boring or slow-kill-me-now paced. There were many ‘lol-worthy’ moments, dialogs and scenes for certain. This novella honestly doesn’t contain exactly my kind of humour or chemistry between characters, so it didn’t make me laugh or swoon, but entertaining is what it was never the less and, if you enjoyed <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17788403.Maybe_Someday__Maybe___1_" title="Maybe Someday (Maybe, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Maybe Someday</a>, then there are good chances this will please you very much. And, thank goodness, there is no love-triangle. It in fact follows the relationship between Warren and Bridgette, how they met and developed this ‘interesting’ and, at first sight, vividly unsettling connection.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5430144.Colleen_Hoover" title="Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Colleen Hoover</a>’s talent at creating appropriate atmospheres is worth a <em>
  <strong>BRAVO!</strong>
</em> She does it like a boss, and you just can’t help but nod your head in agreement. She makes any close to be redundant scene easily and enjoyably readable. I especially approve her choice of point of views in the stories she writes. For instance, this is narrated by Warren and so gives us an insight on how this porn addicted (HA, you will see why), comical, honest and intense guy thinks <em>and what he wants</em>. I’m almost sure that, had this been narrated by Bridgette’s point of view, it would have felt completely different and even more angsty. Which is why I think the author made a great decision here.<br><br>I’m positive the reason why I’m not ‘shipping’ this couple as much as I wish I were is because of Bridgette. She is rude, mean, negative and unpleasant to read about overall. At first, I didn’t mind it all that much, because I really wanted to understand her and maybe sympathize…and I did. For some time. But it’s not because you had a hard life or that you don’t trust men that you’re allowed to act in that way, in my opinion.<br><br>For example, you had a bad day. A damn awful and scream-worthy day. Of course, you will feel negative and grumpy but that doesn’t mean you have to take it all on people. It could be understandable, but not pleasant still. I know it’s not the same thing, but I wanted to help you visualize how I just think that, if the person isn’t the cause of your problems, he/she doesn’t deserve that attitude. I know it’s not easy, but I wanted her to try harder. Alright, I admit that Warren wasn’t an angel and maybe I would have started by acting the same as Bridgette around him in the first three chapters or so, but not for quite as long as she in reality does. He just, sigh, changed and her noticeable character development was too far into the story for me to ignore everything that happened before. But, hey, he likes mean girls, as he clearly stated in the book, so if he’s not complaining, then I’ll let them have their happily-ever-after. And it’s not that I hate her: she’s simply not the kind of character I enjoy reading about in a book apparently.<br><br>The writing was good. It did contain some minor but noticeable repetitions though. Warren was smirk-worthy and likeable, Bridgette not that much, like I said, and the secondary characters fantastic and rightly appearing when they needed to! There aren’t many events, since this <em>is</em> a novella and focuses on the ‘original’ couple. The atmosphere, of course, fabulous and the story overall nicely done. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5430144.Colleen_Hoover" title="Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Colleen Hoover</a> really may be an author I’m not necessarily exclusively praising, but I still can’t help but read her novels. She’s a guilty pleasure of mine. I’m a little sad I couldn’t connect with Bridgette as I strongly hoped to though, having found her intriguing in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17788403.Maybe_Someday__Maybe___1_" title="Maybe Someday (Maybe, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Maybe Someday</a>, but I nevertheless have no regrets for having picked this short story up. Happy reading!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15704249236210422190" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

</a><br/><br/>Colleen Hoover surprised us with this novella, and in the best way! If you’ve read <i>Maybe Someday</i>, you know Warren. Warren was the most memorable and also my favorite character from that book. He’s like Daniel from <i>Losing Hope</i>. One of those side characters you just have to know more about. I am so thankful that CoHo decided to give us a little something from his perspective! His story with Bridgett. <br/><br/>Being in Warren’s head was a treat. He is just hilario</span>
  <span id="freeText17103474664350388855" style="display:none"><b>5 ‘Haven’t met the right asshole’ stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/96912f58-07cd-4b31-a549-8fb269319aa5_zps13d0f92a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416919100i/12116405.jpg" alt=" photo 96912f58-07cd-4b31-a549-8fb269319aa5_zps13d0f92a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Colleen Hoover surprised us with this novella, and in the best way! If you’ve read <i>Maybe Someday</i>, you know Warren. Warren was the most memorable and also my favorite character from that book. He’s like Daniel from <i>Losing Hope</i>. One of those side characters you just have to know more about. I am so thankful that CoHo decided to give us a little something from his perspective! His story with Bridgett. <br><br>Being in Warren’s head was a treat. He is just hilarious, yet sweet and sexy at the same time. I knew I would love him even more in this, and I was right. Then there is Bridgett. The things I remember most about Bridgett is that she works at Hooters, she’s kind of bitchy, and has a love hate relationship with Warren. I’m glad we got a little more insight on what is going on in her life. And I’m also glad we found out what was up with Warren’s porn fascination. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/93b30cef-8e95-4660-8c0b-ce63096b6727_zpsa416b711.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Warren and Bridgett start as roommates thrown in together unwillingly. Then things change between them. It’s hard to describe. Are they friends? Boyfriend/girlfriend? Is it just sex? Or is more brewing between them....<br><br><i>Maybe Not</i> is a quick and fun read I highly recommend for fans of <i>Maybe Someday</i>. It’s full of humor, but it also has an emotional side. And Colleen Hoover brought the heat in this one! I loved the steamy scenes. The writing was fantastic (I knew it would be) and the only thing I would change is that I wanted more! A novella just wasn't enough for these characters. I'm greedy. I wanted a full length book ;) <br> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/2babc017-fb94-46ed-b1e6-6375840ce3da_zpse18efa38.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><i>

    <blockquote> “She’s nothing I’ve ever wanted in a girl. And absolutely everything I need.”</blockquote>

<div id="review_1110548969" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1110548969" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1110548969?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1110548969" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2008715215369089520"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416862576i/12084394.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“She’s nothing I’ve ever wanted… And absolutely everything I need.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/>This was a fun, sexy surprise treat from Colleen Hoover giving fans of Maybe Someday a look into the love, pranks, and general hilarity of Warren’s life as he falls for the last girl he ever thought he could love.<br/><br/>While you can certainly read this spin-off novella on it’s own, I personally would highly recommend reading Maybe Someday first. Not only does that book tell a gorgeous, unique love story, but it’s also one o</span>
  <span id="freeText2008715215369089520" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416862576i/12084394.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“She’s nothing I’ve ever wanted… And absolutely everything I need.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>This was a fun, sexy surprise treat from Colleen Hoover giving fans of Maybe Someday a look into the love, pranks, and general hilarity of Warren’s life as he falls for the last girl he ever thought he could love.<br><br>While you can certainly read this spin-off novella on it’s own, I personally would highly recommend reading Maybe Someday first. Not only does that book tell a gorgeous, unique love story, but it’s also one of my all-time favorite 5-star standalones. A top recommendation for every single romance reader.<br><br>I read this in one sitting! I don’t want to tell you too much about it though because it’s a quick read and I think it’ll be way more fun to just discover it for yourself!! For anyone who doesn’t remember, Warren is one of Ridge’s close friends and his roommate. When Bridgette comes to live in their house, his whole life is turned upside down by this angry girl who invades his bathroom and seems to hate him.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I feel like I’m two different people right now. I’m a guy who finds his new roommate insanely attractive, but I’m also a guy who can’t stand to be around his bitchy new roommate.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>But this doesn’t deter him. One prank leads to another, and then one kiss leads to so much more…<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “I can’t inhale, no matter how hard I try, because the need to kiss her has taken over… I need her air. I kiss her so desperately, I forget that I’m still mad at her.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>The sparks flew and this fun enemies-to-lovers novella kept me smiling. Maybe Not shows us a light-hearted, sexy side of Colleen Hoover’s writing and is a real treat for fans of Maybe Someday! :)<br><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/586236988" rel="nofollow noopener">Click here for my review of Maybe Someday.</a><br>_______________________________________<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14426631938573890204">English - Español <br/><br/>We knew Warren and Bridgette from Maybe Someday, but here there are a lot of stuff that we didn't have many details.<br/><br/>Here we can learn a little more about Bridgette and her reasons for being the way she is, although I don't like it. It's a little funny. It's amazing Warren's tenacit</span>
  <span id="freeText14426631938573890204" style="display:none">English - Español <br /><br />We knew Warren and Bridgette from Maybe Someday, but here there are a lot of stuff that we didn't have many details.<br /><br />Here we can learn a little more about Bridgette and her reasons for being the way she is, although I don't like it. Having a difficult life doesn't give you the right to pay it with people who are not to blame, but everyone faces problems differently.<br /><br />We learned the reason for the addition of Warren to porn movies. It's a little funny. It's amazing Warren's tenacity to stand Bridgette and try to achieve what he wants from the first moment he saw her: to be in a relationship with her. It was like love at first sight, but everything done upside down, first sex, sex and lots of sex and at the end first date and holding hands.<br /><br />If you read Maybe Someday, and liked Warren as much as I did, then you should read this novel. Above all, it is narrated from his point of view. I think that at this moment everyone should know of my predilection for books narrated by men. They are the best!<br /><br />✨✨✨<br /><br />Ya conocíamos a Warren y Bridgette desde Maybe Someday, pero aquí se abunda mucho en cosas que no teníamos muchos detalles.<br /><br />Aquí podemos conocer un poco más a Bridgette y sus razones para ser como es, aunque no lo comparto. El haber tenido una vida difícil no te da derecho a pagarlo con personas que no tienen la culpa, pero cada quien afronta los problemas de manera diferente.<br /><br />Nos enteramos de la razón de la adición de Warren a películas pornograficas. Es un poco gracioso. Es increíble la tenacidad de Warren para soportar a Bridgette y tratar de lograr lo que él quiere desde el primer momento que la vio: estar en una relación con ella. Fue algo como amor a primera vista, pero todo hecho al revés, primero sexo, sexo y mucho sexo y al final primera cita y tomarse de las manos. <br /><br />Si leíste Maybe Someday, y Warren te gustó tanto como a mí, entonces no debes dejar de leer esta novela. Sobretodo que está narrada desde su punto de vista. Creo que a este momento todos deben saber de mi predilección por libros narrados por hombres. Son lo mejor!</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=top-fantasy-boyfriends">top-fantasy-boyfriends</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1110278259" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15832617120349576936"><b>*****FIVE STARS*****</b><br/>{BR with Mel, Sharon, and Tiff}<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/d3f4c3c60c789a4de6da1857819ccf8f_zps00e13c8c.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416973445i/12142082._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo d3f4c3c60c789a4de6da1857819ccf8f_zps00e13c8c.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>I absolutely loved this little novella!!<br/>When I read <b>"Maybe Someday"</b>, I remember really loving Warren. Any guy who is gorgeous and also has an amazing sense of humor, is beyond sexy. I have to admit, I loved him a helluva lot more than Ridge's character.<br/><br/><br/><br/><b>"Maybe Not"</b> is Warren and Bridgette's story. We never really got Bridgette's back story in the previous book, and in this one we learn she may have a possible connection to one of the roommate</span>
  <span id="freeText15832617120349576936" style="display:none"><b>*****FIVE STARS*****</b><br>{BR with Mel, Sharon, and Tiff}<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/d3f4c3c60c789a4de6da1857819ccf8f_zps00e13c8c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416973445i/12142082._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo d3f4c3c60c789a4de6da1857819ccf8f_zps00e13c8c.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I absolutely loved this little novella!!<br>When I read <b>"Maybe Someday"</b>, I remember really loving Warren. Any guy who is gorgeous and also has an amazing sense of humor, is beyond sexy. I have to admit, I loved him a helluva lot more than Ridge's character.<br><br><br><br><b>"Maybe Not"</b> is Warren and Bridgette's story. We never really got Bridgette's back story in the previous book, and in this one we learn she may have a possible connection to one of the roommates. Bridgette definitely has a lot of anger management issues but we learn that she has had a pretty hard life and has never been in a loving environment.<br><br><br><br>Warren is instantly attracted to Bridgette, not only for her looks, but he's drawn to her mean girl attitude. He is perceived as shallow but in actuality this guy has the ability to see there is so much more to this girl and he makes it his mission to break through her walls.<br><br><br><b>She's so confusing. She's so frustrating. She's so damn unpredictable. She's nothing I ever wanted in a girl. And absolutely everything I need.</b><br><br><br><br>I loved all of his inner monologues and I'm glad that we learn why he was always watching porn, because I thought that was so odd when reading the previous book. The reason is pretty hysterical.<br><br><br><br>Now I have to mention the sexy times. They were <b>OFF THE CHARTS HOT</b>!!Panties will be melting while reading this one.<br><br><br>My only complaint is that I wish COHO had made it a full length novel instead of such a short novella. </span>

<div id="review_1111179926" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1111179926" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406624675p2/31339793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1111179926?book_show_action=true">Nov 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=all-time-fav-author">all-time-fav-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=fluffy-fluffer">fluffy-fluffer</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=laugh-out-loud">laugh-out-loud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=oh-look-pretty-cover">oh-look-pretty-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=killing-me-with-sexual-tension">killing-me-with-sexual-tension</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=smartass-witty-banters">smartass-witty-banters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=standalones">standalones</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=swoon-worthy-guys">swoon-worthy-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=i-love-me-some-angst-drama">i-love-me-some-angst-drama</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1111179926" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1035875169320899168"><b>4 WARREN STARS! ★★★★</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416841601i/12080565.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"She's the best worst thing that's ever happened to me."</i>
</b><br/><br/><b><u>Jasmine Trivia 101</u>:</b> Whatever this lady writes, I read it as soon as it releases <s>even at the expense of my job</s>. <b>Colleen Hoover</b> is my "drop everything right now to read" author and even if I didn't love <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17788401.Ugly_Love' title='Ugly Love by Colleen Hoover' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ugly Love</a>, <b>my faith in this author never wavers.</b> So imagine my surprise when this was dropped out of nowhere and when I heard it featured my most fav character from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17788403.Maybe_Someday__Maybe___1_' title='Maybe Someday (Maybe, #1) by Colleen Hoover' rel='nofollow noopener'>Maybe Someday</a>, EVERYTHING IN LIFE IS PUT ON HOLD AND I</span>
  <span id="freeText1035875169320899168" style="display:none"><b>4 WARREN STARS! ★★★★</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416841601i/12080565.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"She's the best worst thing that's ever happened to me."</i>
</b><br><br><b><u>Jasmine Trivia 101</u>:</b> Whatever this lady writes, I read it as soon as it releases <s>even at the expense of my job</s>. <b>Colleen Hoover</b> is my "drop everything right now to read" author and even if I didn't love <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17788401.Ugly_Love" title="Ugly Love by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Ugly Love</a>, <b>my faith in this author never wavers.</b> So imagine my surprise when this was dropped out of nowhere and when I heard it featured my most fav character from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17788403.Maybe_Someday__Maybe___1_" title="Maybe Someday (Maybe, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Maybe Someday</a>, EVERYTHING IN LIFE IS PUT ON HOLD AND I DO A HAPPY DANCE. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397909858ra/9344915.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you've read Maybe Someday and have already met Warren and fell in love with him like I did, then <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23587984.Maybe_Not__Maybe___1_5_" title="Maybe Not (Maybe, #1.5) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Maybe Not</a> is CoHo's way of sending you that early Christmas gift you've been dying to get your hands on eventhough you haven't been a nice kid this year ;) On the contrary, this was like a <b>naughty version of Maybe Someday</b> wrapped up with so much humor and wit! <br><br><b>Told entirely from Warren's POV, this book NEVER had a dull moment.</b> We all remembered Warren as being the master prankster and for his endless porn-watching days (psst, there's a reason for this *winks*), but being in his head definitely opened up a whole new side to him. I loved how shamelessly entertaining his thoughts were and there was no shying away from his cocky, ego-boosting ways which just made me love him so much more. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"If you have sex with me, Bridgette, you're the one in danger of becoming clingy. You'll want so much of me, I won't be able to tell the difference between you and Saran Wrap."</i>
</blockquote><br>And there's <b>Bridgette</b> who let's admit, didn't exactly leave as good as much of an impression in MS but in this one, readers will finally get to see more of her and boy, is she one hard nut to crack! <b>She definitely challenged Warren in more ways than one that brought out the steam factor to a CoHo all-time high!</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399699398ra/9584343.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Of course with a novella, the main challenge is being the relationship build-up and while I definitely wished for more (note: the book ends at 80% mark), CoHo still played out Warren &amp; Bridgette's relationship <b>with just the right pace without coming off completely rushed or unrealistic.</b> There are times where it leaves you a little frustrated but sooner than later, you can't help but fall for these endearing characters. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“The only difference between falling in love and being in love is that your heart already knows how you feel, but your mind is too stubborn to admit it.”</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415443863i/11789676.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In a true CoHo fashion, <u>Maybe Not</u> was a <b>nice quick heart-warming read packaged together with a swoon-worthy male lead and an added bonus of humor with some steam to go along.</b> After being letdown by her previous work, this one definitely redeemed it for me &amp; I absolutely devoured it within hours! <br><br>And while this is a spinoff novella of Maybe Someday, I'd like to emphasize that <b>it's NOT a rehash of that aforementioned book</b> :)<br><br><i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23587984.Maybe_Not__Maybe___1_5_" title="Maybe Not (Maybe, #1.5) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Maybe Not</a> is a spinoff novella of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17788403.Maybe_Someday__Maybe___1_" title="Maybe Someday (Maybe, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Maybe Someday</a> and while it can be read as a standalone, it would be recommended to be read after the first book.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="1035875169320899168" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1110648117" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10812657677821111632"><b>4.5 <i>Warren is a definite yes</i> Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416881316i/12098810._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I loved <i>Maybe Someday</i>, so when I saw we would get Warren’s story, even if it was a novella, I was so excited. I already loved Warren and now I love him even more. We saw the dynamic between Bridgette and Warren, but I had no idea how funny they both are. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>"You kiss like you’re trying to resuscitate a dead cate."<br/><br/>"You kiss like you are a dead cat.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Their banter had me laughing out loud. In the novella we see the ins and outs of why Bridgette came to live with Wa</span>
  <span id="freeText10812657677821111632" style="display:none"><b>4.5 <i>Warren is a definite yes</i> Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416881316i/12098810._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved <i>Maybe Someday</i>, so when I saw we would get Warren’s story, even if it was a novella, I was so excited. I already loved Warren and now I love him even more. We saw the dynamic between Bridgette and Warren, but I had no idea how funny they both are. <br><br><b>
  <i>"You kiss like you’re trying to resuscitate a dead cate."<br><br>"You kiss like you are a dead cat.”</i>
</b><br><br>Their banter had me laughing out loud. In the novella we see the ins and outs of why Bridgette came to live with Warren and Ridge. The story begins before Sydney moves in and we see how Warren’s porn addiction started, and so much more.<br><br>A lot times a bitchy heroine can get annoying, but this is short and Bridgette just kept growing on me. Yes, Bridgette is a bitch and comes off a little harsh, and Warren comes off like an egoistical asshole…hey it works!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416881316i/12098811._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved how steamy things were between Bridgette and Warren. I loved how Warren helped Bridgette find a home and family. I love how throughout it all these two remained true to themselves. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416881316i/12098812._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This is such a fun read. I highly recommend reading this one, if you read and enjoyed Maybe Someday. <br></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1110217615" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10853362146067140188">4--<b>Bitchin'</b>--Stars!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"She’s so confusing. She’s so frustrating. She’s so damn unpredictable.<br/>She’s nothing I’ve ever wanted in a girl. And absolutely everything I need."</blockquote>
  </i>

<span id="freeTextContainer11754210314757757081"><b> 3.5 stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “It’s hard to fall in love with assholes, Warren.”..<br/>“Maybe you just haven’t met the right asshole yet.” </i> </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/maybenot.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>This was super cute!!!!!! I wasn't the biggest fan of Maybe Someday, but when I read so many positive reviews on this novella, I had to give it a shot and I'm glad I did! I ended up like it more than Maybe Someday.<br/><br/>Maybe Not is the short story of Ridge and Sydney's roommates, Warren and Bridgette. In this we get to see how they meet, how an attraction builds and then eventual</span>
  <span id="freeText11754210314757757081" style="display:none"><b> 3.5 stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> “It’s hard to fall in love with assholes, Warren.”..<br>“Maybe you just haven’t met the right asshole yet.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/maybenot.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417682124i/12487143.png" alt=" photo maybenot.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was super cute!!!!!! I wasn't the biggest fan of Maybe Someday, but when I read so many positive reviews on this novella, I had to give it a shot and I'm glad I did! I ended up like it more than Maybe Someday.<br><br>Maybe Not is the short story of Ridge and Sydney's roommates, Warren and Bridgette. In this we get to see how they meet, how an attraction builds and then eventually a sexual relationship (and boy do these two hit the sack). There isn't much in terms of a hard plot, but it did focus on the building of a relationship between two people and I really enjoyed reading their journey.<br><br>Not much more to say except this book is good for some laughs and for some feels. I highly recommend if you need something light yet fulfilling to read.<br><br><b> <i> “The only difference between falling in love and being in love is that your heart already knows how you feel, but your mind is too stubborn to admit it.” </i> </b></span>

    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1121969555?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1121969555" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16689952212346680537"><b>3 Maybe Not stars!</b><br/><blockquote>
  <b>“The only difference between falling in love and being in love is that your heart already knows how you feel, but your mind is too stubborn to admit it.”</b>
</blockquote><br/>This one was a bit of mix bag for me. On the one hand, I like the whole enemie-to-lovers premise, but it also felt too juvenile for my taste. <br/><br/>Major kudos for writing a hero who is totally gone for the heroine this time around though. Two of CoHo's latest books involved heroes who were hung up on other girls instead of the h</span>
  <span id="freeText16689952212346680537" style="display:none"><b>3 Maybe Not stars!</b><br /><blockquote>
  <b>“The only difference between falling in love and being in love is that your heart already knows how you feel, but your mind is too stubborn to admit it.”</b>
</blockquote><br />This one was a bit of mix bag for me. On the one hand, I like the whole enemie-to-lovers premise, but it also felt too juvenile for my taste. <br /><br />Major kudos for writing a hero who is totally gone for the heroine this time around though. Two of CoHo's latest books involved heroes who were hung up on other girls instead of the heroine, so Warren being totally, obviously in love with Bridgette was a refreshing change. I just wasn't as invested in their story as I was with others though. I don't know if it's the length or the fact that I never got to know Bridgette that much.<br /><br />But overall, this was a good novella. CoHo fans will surely loved this one but it's just okay for me. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16689952212346680537" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1131101749?book_show_action=true">Dec 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela" href="/user/show/30035966-angela">Angela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30035966-angela?shelf=5-star-favorites">5-star-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30035966-angela?shelf=read-it-and-weep">read-it-and-weep</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1131101749" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11605787659363145302"><b> 5 out of 5 perfect asshole stars</b> <br/><br/><i>Maybe Not</i> is the novella for <a href='http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/2014/12/maybe-someday-by-colleen-hoover.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <i>Maybe Someday</i>
</a> (<i>Maybe </i>1.5). This book follows <br/>Warren, Ridges roommate, and Bridgette who is also their roommate. <br/>Warren was actually my favorite character in the first book and I was so<br/> happy to get a story from his pov. In the first book I was always wanting to hear more about him,  and felt we never got to truly meet him. <br/><br/>I absolutely loved being able to get inside his head. I love hearing all <br/>his cocky, comical, and real emotio</span>
  <span id="freeText11605787659363145302" style="display:none"><b> 5 out of 5 perfect asshole stars</b> <br><br><i>Maybe Not</i> is the novella for <a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/2014/12/maybe-someday-by-colleen-hoover.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <i>Maybe Someday</i>
</a> (<i>Maybe </i>1.5). This book follows <br>Warren, Ridges roommate, and Bridgette who is also their roommate. <br>Warren was actually my favorite character in the first book and I was so<br> happy to get a story from his pov. In the first book I was always wanting to hear more about him,  and felt we never got to truly meet him. <br><br>I absolutely loved being able to get inside his head. I love hearing all <br>his cocky, comical, and real emotions. Getting to hear Bridgette's <br>story was a breath of fresh air as well. Since all we really knew about her in book one was that shes was a super b. (<i>Oh and I don't wanna forget that we find out what Warren's obsession with porn is all about and <b>I LOVED LOVED LOVED</b> the reason behind it! So freaking hilarious.</i> <i>Yeah, never thought those words would come out of my mouth</i>.) Getting to see how their relationship got started before Sydney moved in made a few of those unanswered question from book one so crystal. The banter between the two is what makes this book so unstoppable. It's has the brass and balls most novellas can't seem to master. I can't thank Hoover enough for keeping Warren the same silly ass as he was in the first book. <b>Just loved him so much!<br><br><div><br></div>
<br><div>
<br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-r9-CbDN2vTo/VNlIQMey10I/AAAAAAAABMg/ImGqfVHEvUQ/s1600/asshole.gif" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423526744ra/13638513.gif" height="131" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</div>
<br><div>
<br><br>Getting to experience the relationship between Warren and Bridgette might just be the biggest treat I get all year! Their relationship truly is like no other and it had me falling hard. UGH words haven't been invented yet for how I feel about this book!!! This is a quick, witty, and hilariously entertaining story. If it wouldn't have been for the ending of <i>Maybe Someday</i>, <i>Maybe Not</i> would be in a side by side tie. (Because you can't beat <i>Someday</i>'s ending). I will say the ending to this book too was just so perfect! <b>Can't stress how <br>much I loved this book!!!<br><br><b>I fell in love with you warren and I'm <br>not sorry about it. </b><br><br>I wish this book would have been a full length novel... Who knows maybe well get more later. <br><br><b> READ THIS REVIEW AND OTHERS OVER ON OUR BLOG: <br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/">http://southernbredsouthernread.blogs...</a><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/">http://southernbredsouthernread.blogs...</a><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/">http://southernbredsouthernread.blogs...</a><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/">http://southernbredsouthernread.blogs...</a></b></b>
</div></b></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1855021035" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12398123784274923165">I know, I know!!! I’m the last person to finally read this one. I read <u>Maybe Someday</u> in 2013 and <b>MAYBE NOT</b> was released in 2014 and here it is almost 2017 and I’m finally reading this one. *hangs head in shame* <br/><br/>We met Bridgette and Warren in <u>Maybe Someday</u> and ever since we’ve got a glimpse of these two I’ve wanted their story. Ms. Hoover didn’t disappoint by providing her fans with this novella. <b>Maybe Not</b> parallels Maybe Someday so a lot of blanks are filled in on what was happening between Brid</span>
  <span id="freeText12398123784274923165" style="display:none">I know, I know!!! I’m the last person to finally read this one. I read <u>Maybe Someday</u> in 2013 and <b>MAYBE NOT</b> was released in 2014 and here it is almost 2017 and I’m finally reading this one. *hangs head in shame* <br><br>We met Bridgette and Warren in <u>Maybe Someday</u> and ever since we’ve got a glimpse of these two I’ve wanted their story. Ms. Hoover didn’t disappoint by providing her fans with this novella. <b>Maybe Not</b> parallels Maybe Someday so a lot of blanks are filled in on what was happening between Bridgette and Warren. Plus, the best part is the story is told in Warren’s pov. <br><blockquote>
  <b>“Mean girls are my weakness.” -Warren</b>
</blockquote><br>Bridgette seems incapable of being nice to anyone. Hearing the reason why she has a hardened outer core helps make her more likable. I loved that Warren was attracted to her even though she was a tough nut to crack. <br><br>Their relationship was totally backward. They had sexy times long before they even held hands but that is what worked between these two. <br><br>I listened to the audio version. There are few odd spots where the narrator's voice changes. Like they had a voice over. It only happens a couple times so it doesn’t affect my enjoyment of the story. <br><br>If you’ve read Maybe Someday then you need to grab this book and read it. It is an entertaining quick story that shouldn’t be missed by those who loved Warren.<br><br><b>SERIES</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24445517.Maybe_Someday__Maybe___1_" title="Maybe Someday (Maybe, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1421002815s/24445517.jpg" alt="Maybe Someday (Maybe, #1) by Colleen Hoover" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Novella</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23587984.Maybe_Not__Maybe___1_5_" title="Maybe Not (Maybe, #1.5) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1416381591s/23587984.jpg" alt="Maybe Not (Maybe, #1.5) by Colleen Hoover" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://foxyblogs.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442610494i/16258382._SX540_.jpg" width="400" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1110215743" />
    <a title="Sophie&#39;s Reading Corner " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33135672-sophie-s-reading-corner"><img alt="Sophie&#39;s Reading Corner " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587591372p2/33135672.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1110215743?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophie&#39;s Reading Corner " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophie&#39;s Reading Corner " href="/user/show/33135672-sophie-s-reading-corner">Sophie&#39;s Reading Corner </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33135672-sophie-s-reading-corner?shelf=most-anticipated">most-anticipated</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1110215743" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10015186024069765005"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416875745i/12096938._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/> <i>
  <b>“It’s hard to fall in love with assholes, Warren.”<br/> “Maybe you just haven’t met the right asshole yet.” </b>
</i><br/><br/>Maybe Not was a really fun & sweet read. It's a novella & a spin off from Maybe Someday & I can't describe how excited I was when I heard that we'd have a book about Warren & Bridget. Warren was one of the best characters in Maybe Someday. I loved him so much & I was very excited when I realised that this was written from his POV. <br/><br/>I loved that a couple of things that happened in Maybe Some</span>
  <span id="freeText10015186024069765005" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416875745i/12096938._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <i>
  <b>“It’s hard to fall in love with assholes, Warren.”<br> “Maybe you just haven’t met the right asshole yet.” </b>
</i><br><br>Maybe Not was a really fun &amp; sweet read. It's a novella &amp; a spin off from Maybe Someday &amp; I can't describe how excited I was when I heard that we'd have a book about Warren &amp; Bridget. Warren was one of the best characters in Maybe Someday. I loved him so much &amp; I was very excited when I realised that this was written from his POV. <br><br>I loved that a couple of things that happened in Maybe Someday were somehow explained in this one. Like for example the reason behind Warren's porn obsession or Bridgette's personality &amp; of course their relationship. <br><br>I have to admit that it made me laugh &amp; I was in awe a couple of times. Warren is a really entertaining character and his banter with Bridgette was gold! I was so anticipating to read about their hot angry-sexy moments, because I was expecting them, judging always by their apparent relationship in Maybe Someday. <br><br> <i>
  <b>“You kiss like you’re trying to resuscitate a dead cat,” she says, disgusted.<br> “You kiss like you are a dead cat.” <br> “You probably fuck like a limp noodle.”<br> “I fuck like I’m Thor.” </b>
</i><br><br>Thankfully, overall I wasn't disappointed, but the ending.. It was just too sudden. It finished way too early for my taste &amp; I wished we had a little bit more, you know? <br><br><b>PS:</b>I don't know why, but Warren reminds me of another beloved character, Griffin from the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13517535.Thoughtless__Thoughtless___1_" title="Thoughtless (Thoughtless, #1) by S.C. Stephens" rel="nofollow noopener">Thoughtless</a> series. Maybe they are nothing alike, but I enjoy both of them &amp; looking forward to reading Griffin's book, when it comes out, next year. </span>

    <a title="Glass" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4808910-glass"><img alt="Glass" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583244629p2/4808910.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1110189750?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Glass" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Glass" href="/user/show/4808910-glass">Glass</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808910-glass?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808910-glass?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808910-glass?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808910-glass?shelf=fangirling-like-crazy">fangirling-like-crazy</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1110189750" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17930018734448137750"><b>Review posted at <a href='http://jacitamati.blogspot.com/2014/12/maybe-not-maybe-someday-15-by-colleen.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ja čitam, a ti?</a></b><br/><br/> First I have to say that I am not usually fan of novellas - almost every single one I've read so far was only there to fill time between book one and book two, or to remind people to buy "original" book. They don't bring anything new or fairly important, I end up cursing myself for even picking them up. This did not happen with this release. <br/><br/> <i>Maybe Not</i> is a story about Warren and Bridgette, secondary characters from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17788403.Maybe_Someday__Maybe___1_' title='Maybe Someday (Maybe, #1) by Colleen Hoover' rel='nofollow noopener'>Maybe Someday</a>. The odd couple. The crazy ones w</span>
  <span id="freeText17930018734448137750" style="display:none"><b>Review posted at <a href="http://jacitamati.blogspot.com/2014/12/maybe-not-maybe-someday-15-by-colleen.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Ja čitam, a ti?</a></b><br /><br /> First I have to say that I am not usually fan of novellas - almost every single one I've read so far was only there to fill time between book one and book two, or to remind people to buy "original" book. They don't bring anything new or fairly important, I end up cursing myself for even picking them up. This did not happen with this release. <br /><br /> <i>Maybe Not</i> is a story about Warren and Bridgette, secondary characters from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17788403.Maybe_Someday__Maybe___1_" title="Maybe Someday (Maybe, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Maybe Someday</a>. The odd couple. The crazy ones who made us laugh. I am so happy that Colleen Hoover decided to surprise us with their story no matter how short it is. I do wish there were more pages, but this was okay too. Better something than nothing, right? <br /><br /><br /> <blockquote>
  <i>"I don't want you to change Bridgette. I'm not in love with who you could be, or who you used to be, or who the world thinks you should be. I'm in love with you. Right now. Just like this."</i>
</blockquote><br /><br /><b>All the reasons to read <i>Maybe Not</i>:</b><br /><br /><br /> <b>- That quote above.</b> If you want more, just read it. I highlighted whole thing in the end. <br /><br /> <b>- Quick, but satisfying read.</b> Unlike many others novellas, you do not feel as if anything is rushed. This is not continuation of the previous novel trough the perspective of other characters. Timeline is the same like in Maybe Someday, but focus of the story is on completely different events. There are couple of scenes you will recognize, but still it is like you are reading them for the first time.<br /> <br /> <b>- Warren.</b> Oh my God, Warren! Tanja can we squeeze him into your harem somehow? Do not worry, I will take care of him. <br /> <br /> <b>- Hotness overload.</b> But seriously! Colleen Hoover, I didn't know you had it in you. You should definitely write steamier scenes more often. I know that some of you (still) aren't comfortable with reading explicit scenes, so consider this as a warning - Maybe Not is most definitely 18+ read. <br /><br /> <b>- I walked on the clouds all day.</b> Every once in a while we all need one of those "feel good", happy and fluffy reads.<br /><br /> <br /> In the end, other than trying to make you read this, I will share just one more quote with you. If this doesn't work out, than you have cold, cold hart. <br /><br /> <blockquote>
  <i>"I press my lips to hers with such delicacy; I want her to feel everything she's ever deserved to feel at the hands of someone else. She deserves to feel beautiful. She deserves to feel important. She deserves to feel cared for. She deserves to feel respected. She deserves to feel like there's at least one other person in this world who accepts her for exactly who she is.<br /> She deserves to know how I feel. because I feel all of those things. And maybe a little more."</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Read my review for <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/749950296?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Maybe Someday</a>
</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17930018734448137750" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1110408501" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1110408501" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1110408501?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1110408501" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7944759341205134592"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/598376.gif' width='400' height='250' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This novella about Warren and Bridgette is just <i>really sweet</i>. I know, I know...it doesn't really seem like it since they both pretend to pretty much hate each other but it's not like that at all. <br/><br/>Warren sees something in Bridgette right from the beginning. Sure he has a "thing" for mean girls but it's something more, not insta-love, just a desire to get to know the <b>
  <i>real</i>
</b> Bridgette. It certainly helps that we get his POV. <br/><br/>And it doesn't help that we don't get Bridgette's. We never really know </span>
  <span id="freeText7944759341205134592" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/598376.gif" width="400" height="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This novella about Warren and Bridgette is just <i>really sweet</i>. I know, I know...it doesn't really seem like it since they both pretend to pretty much hate each other but it's not like that at all. <br><br>Warren sees something in Bridgette right from the beginning. Sure he has a "thing" for mean girls but it's something more, not insta-love, just a desire to get to know the <b>
  <i>real</i>
</b> Bridgette. It certainly helps that we get his POV. <br><br>And it doesn't help that we don't get Bridgette's. We never really know what she's thinking. Thankfully, we get little tidbits along the way but Bridgette has some serious reasons why she's a mean girl. <br><br>There's a lot of steaminess in this one. CH certainly didn't hold back. These two get to business right from the get-go and at first, it's just a physical thing but then it becomes so much more. I really enjoyed reading about how it developed. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/489227.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved all the pranks between the roommates but the pepper juice has to be the best. My heart went out for Warren on the last one though...that was a bit tough. But I really enjoyed their sarcastic banter with each other.<br><br>I loved getting a little bit of Sydney and Ridge. I just wish there was more...a lot more. In fact, I would have loved this "surprise" novella to have been about them! <br><br>But back to Warren and Bridgette. Another favorite scene was the one at Warren's sisters. The parts with Conner and Bridgette were priceless. Brody wasn't too bad either. <br><br>And it ends really well. I just loved the two beds idea! <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448044472ra/17086030.gif" width="400" height="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>"I hate unicorns and rainbows.” I drop my face to her neck and I start to laugh. “Oh, my God, I can’t believe you’re mine.”</i><br><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ “You kiss like you’re trying to resuscitate a dead cat,” she says, disgusted. <br><br>“You kiss like you <i>are</i> a dead cat.”<br><br>[...]<br><br>“You probably fuck like a limp noodle.” <br><br>“I fuck like I’m Thor.”<br><br>♥ “You <i>did</i> smile, Bridgette,” I whisper. “And you need to own it, because it was fucking beautiful.”<br><br>♥ "Maybe you just haven't met the right asshole yet." <br><br>♥ “The only difference between <i>falling</i> in love and <i>being</i> in love is that your heart already knows how you feel, but your mind is too stubborn to admit it.” Then I whisper in her ear. “But take all the time you need. I have nothing but patience for you.”<br> <br>♥ “I have an idea,” I whisper against her hair. <br><br>She shakes her head. “I’m not doing anal.”<br><br>[...]<br><br>“I’m such a whore. I already moved in with you and we haven’t even been on a date?” <br><br>“You’re not a whore,” I say to her with mock reassurance. “We haven’t even had sex . . . <i>oh, wait</i>.” I grimace. “You <i>are</i> such a whore. A huge, slutty whore who wants me to try anal with her tonight.”<br><br><br>♦ BR w/Melissa, Patty &amp; Tiffany!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7944759341205134592" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Taylor Knight" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Taylor Knight" href="/user/show/12627819-taylor-knight">Taylor Knight</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1574779465" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10564605422270606950">I started Maybe Not the day after I finished Maybe Someday so everything was still really fresh in my mind. I thought that wouldn't work in my favor, that maybe I would get bored. However, I think it worked out great. I didn't know what Maybe Not was about before I started it. I thought it might be about Sydney before she met Ridge but it actually takes place at the same time as Maybe Someday and it's in the perspective of Warren. I loved Warren so I was really excited that Maybe Not was about h</span>
  <span id="freeText10564605422270606950" style="display:none">I started Maybe Not the day after I finished Maybe Someday so everything was still really fresh in my mind. I thought that wouldn't work in my favor, that maybe I would get bored. However, I think it worked out great. I didn't know what Maybe Not was about before I started it. I thought it might be about Sydney before she met Ridge but it actually takes place at the same time as Maybe Someday and it's in the perspective of Warren. I loved Warren so I was really excited that Maybe Not was about him. <br />I'm not normally a fan of novellas but I loved this one. I think it was totally relevant and added a lot to the characters of Maybe Someday. I really liked getting to know Warren better and I loved that we get some backstory on Bridgette. I do wish Maybe Not was longer. I would have loved it if it was a full length book. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8110590424553949137">RE-READ<br/><br/><b>4.5 STARS<br/><br/>Warren and Bridgette were an awesome couple.</b><br/><br/><i>'Maybe Not'</i> is fab little novella that packs a punch. It's got a hero who's immature, funny, dry.... and actually kinda sexy and romantic too. Told from entirely Warrens POV we get to see how the behind the scenes couple got together.<br/><br/>I LOVED this couple together.<br/><br/>It has pranks, love/hate, funny one-liners, streamy scenes and strong characters.<br/><br/>What more could i want........?<br/><br/>Oh yeah... more pages.<br/><br/>Dammit.<br/><br/>Gonna miss them.<br/><br/>I ♥ Warren & Bridget</span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('W2uveXCwF3WIn5Hbq0ZG4HFiBQfhJcF8ibzsQE4octTBv8rogkNHV0ZH4Ij3FmNgKhLCJEt+jTOxZdiHlvf00Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('uBBaREzUDOuQzejm93xp2QcWXtystAAelpqB1rm6AiUixD/VvidcyV4VmbWrLExZXGaZ/wbvTFGuQ7URYWWEIA==')})
  }

Colleen Hoover is a writer who first came to bestsellerdom through the back door of self-publishing. Signs of the author\'s spunk and energy fill this novel, which is highly readable, funny in all the right places, but also heart-breaking. Readers who value complex character-development and moral ambiguity won\'t find much to love in Confess, but the novel is a fun and clever story of two very unlucky young people who find redemption in each other.  Confess is romantic story about two young people, Auburn and Owen, who both have difficult pasts they\'d like to keep secret. When Owen hires Auburn to work in his art gallery, their immediate attraction is hard to ignore; for the first time in years, they each feel as if they\'ve found someone who understands them. However, the secrets Auburn is hiding means that she has to stay away from Owen, no matter how impossible that seems.  This companion to Confess also includes the following: • Book Review • Story Setting Analysis of Confess • Story elements you may have missed as we decipher the novel • Details of Characters &amp; Key Character Analysis • Summary of the text, with some analytical comments interspersed • Thought Provoking /or Discussion Questions for both Readers &amp; Book Clubs • Discussion &amp; Analysis of Themes, Symbols… • And Much More!  It is an original and entertaining romance, filled with quirky characters, surprising secrets and clever plot twists. The idea of &quot;confession&quot; is explored at all levels. How much does a confession imply guilt? Are all secrets guilty secrets?
